<div id="review_2046183039" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2046183039" />
    <a title="Ahmed  Ejaz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53694260-ahmed-ejaz"><img alt="Ahmed  Ejaz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598778737p2/53694260.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2046183039?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ahmed  Ejaz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ahmed  Ejaz" href="/user/show/53694260-ahmed-ejaz">Ahmed  Ejaz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53694260-ahmed-ejaz?shelf=2017">2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53694260-ahmed-ejaz?shelf=full-lengths">full-lengths</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2046183039" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6540981605145127433">From the previous book, I had learned the lesson not to love characters too much. That lesson really helped me. Because there were very unexpected deaths I didn't want to happen. <br/>But along this fact, there were addition of characters too.<br/> <br/>Remember my complaint about the characters in the previous book that I didn't like them? This book was essential in that regard. I am beginning to like Jonas and Magnus. For now I like Jonas more than Magnus. But Magnus is improving impressively. I am liking th</span>
  <span id="freeText6540981605145127433" style="display:none">From the previous book, I had learned the lesson not to love characters too much. That lesson really helped me. Because there were very unexpected deaths I didn't want to happen. <br />But along this fact, there were addition of characters too.<br /> <br />Remember my complaint about the characters in the previous book that I didn't like them? This book was essential in that regard. I am beginning to like Jonas and Magnus. For now I like Jonas more than Magnus. But Magnus is improving impressively. I am liking that. Maybe in future I will like him more than Jonas. *Fingers crossed* Cleo is also improving in a likeable manner.<br /><br />As far as plot is concerned, this book is pretty plain in that regard. Not that it's boring. Not at all! It just remains the same though out the book and few times represents in different manner. <br />Well, it goes like this: There is a road King Gaius is very impatient to build though out Mytica to link all the three kingdoms. There are just talks about it that it will lead towards Kindred, four crystals which can give god-like powers to the keeper. But rebels are also rising to get back their kingdom. Mostly they are Paelsians. Their leader is Jonas. Rebels will try hard to defeat King Gaius and try find his week points. <br /><br /><b> <i> Be aware. There are some spoilers ahead. </i> </b><br /><br /><br />=&gt; Another main development is an unexpected marriage of Magnus and Cleo. I thought it wouldn't happen because of the earthquake. But King Gaius! He couldn't see the failure of his plan. His wrath was really frightening when he forced Cleo for the marriage. <br /><br />=&gt; Jonas was foolishly brave. Really! His plans to defeat the king were quite good. But he always underestimated the dangers. That was the very weakness of him I felt. In spite of this, I still liked him. <br /><br />=&gt; Lysandra was an amazing addition to this series. She was brave. Jonas and Lysandra's characters were almost the same. Both were stubborn. But Lys was not a foolhardy. She was rational. That was the only difference. <br /><br />=&gt; There was a character from other place than Mytica. Prince Ashur of a vast empire. He was also interested in Kindred. <br />I thought he would kill Nic because he didn't tell him anything about Kindred. Of course I would think so because it was the pattern of this series. Useless characters had no right to live! But Nic was an exception. I didn't like what Ashur did to him rather than killing him. Why?! Why?! What was the need of doing that?! Why Ashur had to be that way?! T__T I meant no offence. I just didn't feel that necessary. <br /><br /><br />Overall, I still enjoyed this book. Ending was intriguing enough for me to start the next book without any further delay.<br /><br /><br />July 3, 2017</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1544134063" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1544134063?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤  by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/50044222-brittney-reverie-and-ink">Brittney ~ Reverie and Ink</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=my-true-loves-gave-to-meeee">my-true-loves-gave-to-meeee</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1544134063" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6199054104703314077"><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Sometimes, to regain sanity, one had to acknowledge and embrace the madness.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>This week is dreadfully busy for me so I find I won’t have much time to review what I read…..which makes me extremely sad for my beautiful boy, Magnus. I just want him to be happy, poor tortured thing. But I WILL say this:<br/><br/>Since I read the first book in February, every time I think of picking up the second, Magnus is all I see. <b>He is all I think about</b>. He is what I missed the most. And now, here in this book, </span>
  <span id="freeText6199054104703314077" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Sometimes, to regain sanity, one had to acknowledge and embrace the madness.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>This week is dreadfully busy for me so I find I won’t have much time to review what I read…..which makes me extremely sad for my beautiful boy, Magnus. I just want him to be happy, poor tortured thing. But I WILL say this:<br><br>Since I read the first book in February, every time I think of picking up the second, Magnus is all I see. <b>He is all I think about</b>. He is what I missed the most. And now, here in this book, I feel like I <i>truly</i> connected with his surly self-I am a goner. And hey, I hear he gets even better….I don’t know. I don’t know if my heart can take his pain. Who am I kidding. <b>I would walk through fire for this dude</b>. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>He wanted so desperately not to care about this-not to care about <i>anything</i> but finding the Kindred for himself and for Lucia-to be as cold and ruthless as his father found it so easy to be.<br>If only that were possible.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>And just so everyone knows, since I am loving this series so much, I might be coming back and adding stuff here and there since I’m so busy. So…sorry in advance. Whoops.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>The boy nodded. "It's best in the end that a princess marry a prince. I suppose."<br>"Ah. I suppose." Oh, this was deeply unpleasant. Being trapped into meaningless small talk with an idiot had never intrigued him, even on a good day. Which this wasn't.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>MAGNUS! AGH! <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"...You have a kind heart, Magnus. And there's nothing you can do to change that."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>---<br><br>EEEPSSSSSS now I <i>really</i> have the <b>Magnus fever</b>....AND I DON'T WANT TO BE CURED AGHHHH!!! <br><br><a href="http://s1301.photobucket.com/user/ChelseaRoberts3/media/kijkhygtfr_zpsusdvumm0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465222128ra/19327321.gif" alt=" photo kijkhygtfr_zpsusdvumm0.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <span id="freeText5123782730204649179" style="display:none"><b>Re-read, part two, with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2665597993" rel="nofollow noopener">Alison</a>!</b><br /><br /><i>THAT’S HOW YOU END IT?!!!</i> My only saving grace is that I took so long to get to this sequel that all six instalments of this series are already released. <br /><br />Ok wow. So this was a roller coaster of emotions. Honestly, I saw the ratings for this and was quite worried ... what are you lot smoking? This was amazing! I was on the edge of my seat, SO WORRIED for my babies. <br /><br /><b>Cleo</b> is an amazingly brave protagonist. I love her so much. I feel so bad for her, considering everything that she’s been through. <b>Magnus</b>, I also love and feel bad for. He’s had such a rough upbringing and just wants to be loved and ... ok I ship him and Cleo <i>SO HARD</i>. <br /><br />I’m kind of indifferent to <b>Lucia</b> though? I hated her chapters. I literally couldn’t care less about her, so hopefully she’ll become a more endearing character in the future instalments?<br /><br />Regardless, I’m going to start book three now because that was a heck of an abrupt ending!<br /><br /><b>P.S. I read this entire book in <i>THREE HOURS</i>! Yes, folks, it’s THAT ADDICTING!</b><br /><br />RTC ;)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7354355799447743050"><b>2 stars</b><br/><br/>The one redeeming quality of this book is the Super Sexy Scottish accent the narrator gives Magnus. <br/><br/>Otherwise, I am sad to say I actually paid for this.<br/><br/>There are so many things wrong with this book....everything from the themes (exploitation of sexual assault and harrassment) to the meat and bones of the book (terribly written dialogue, horrible character arcs).   <span id="freeText7354355799447743050" style="display:none"><b>2 stars</b><br><br>The one redeeming quality of this book is the Super Sexy Scottish accent the narrator gives Magnus. <br><br>Otherwise, I am sad to say I actually paid for this.<br><br>There are so many things wrong with this book....everything from the themes (exploitation of sexual assault and harrassment) to the meat and bones of the book (terribly written dialogue, horrible character arcs). Is it possible that this book is even worse than the first one? Yes, yes it is. <br><br>I don't think I've ever read such terrible dialogue in a published, POPULAR book. The over-the-top drama was infused with almost every scene, and it was exhausting. I swear a daytime soap opera has a better script than this. The actions of the characters make no sense whatsoever either. This whole book is a never-ending cycle of Person A hating Person B's guts and wanting to murder the shit out of him/her. But, because FEELINGS, Person A ends up falling in looooove with Person B. It's absolutely ridiculous.<br><br>Okay let's meet our characters! And to help you get a good sense of their personalities, I'm attaching a gif that describes them to a T.<br><br>PS: some of my gifs are from General Hospital, which is probably more medically accurate than these books. I'm not bitter..... -_-<br><br>First up, we have our piney fresh smelling "if I only had a brain" Jonas:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498145320ra/23099551.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Next in line, our wishy washy whiney princess Cleo (who everyone is in love with):<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498145320ra/23099552.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's-all-that homeboy Aron:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498145320ra/23099553.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Broody, sexy, morally ambiguous Magnus:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498145321ra/23099554.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jekyll and Hyde Lucia:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498145321ra/23099555.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Her bitch Alexius:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498145321ra/23099556.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>The loyal puppy dog Brion:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498145321ra/23099557.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Katniss's sister from another mister Lysandra:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498145321ra/23099558.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Psycho serial killer King Gaius:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1498145321ra/23099559.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>And that's just the main cast geesh. Rhodes needs to trim off the number of characters. This is getting ridiculous.<br><br>Okay overall, the ONLY reason I gave this book 2 stars is because the narrator is awesome. I read the first 2/3 and listened to the last 1/3 when I was taking a road trip. I hated Magnus and his actions/thoughts/feelings, but the narrator totally changed my mind on that. Giving him an accent and inflection definitely made me see Magnus in a whole new light. Sadly, this only worked for Magnus. My opinion stayed the same for the rest of the characters.<br><br>Yes I will be reading the third book, because our fantasy league is the bomb.com and I have so much fun discussing and roasting the books with them =)<br>--------<br><br>Moving along with the Fantasy League!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15747058853292393379">2.5/5 stars<br/><br/>I have a feeling this series just isn't for me. It has a lot of potential and elements that could be amazing but just don't follow through.<br/>The audiobook narrator is fantastic and part of the reason I stuck with this, but the story just hasn't been compelling enough to grip me and keep me wanting more. (It probably didn't help that I read a torch against the night while listening to this audiobook because torch was AMAZING)<br/>For the most part I really enjoy the characters and the fact th</span>
  <span id="freeText15747058853292393379" style="display:none">2.5/5 stars<br /><br />I have a feeling this series just isn't for me. It has a lot of potential and elements that could be amazing but just don't follow through.<br />The audiobook narrator is fantastic and part of the reason I stuck with this, but the story just hasn't been compelling enough to grip me and keep me wanting more. (It probably didn't help that I read a torch against the night while listening to this audiobook because torch was AMAZING)<br />For the most part I really enjoy the characters and the fact that they are very flawed, but I just don't feel an attachment to them. I'm interested, but not enough to NEED to know what happens to them. <br />The story is about the same for me. I'm interested, but not enough to keep going with the series at this point in time. It's just not interesting enough to hold my attention.<br />I totally understand why people love this series, but I just don't.</span>

    <a title="Jiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10502567-jiana"><img alt="Jiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540380229p2/10502567.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781595145925" href="/book/show/18668021-rebel-spring">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1898034411" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17744541850214161299"><b>*yells for the next 10 years* THAT WAS JUST INCREDIBLE.</b><br/><br/>I lowkey stared at my laptop screen for a long while before I actually started typing out my review. I was too shook to write a review for book one and I'm also shook about this one, but I feel the need to write one. Excuse me, it will basically consist of me yelling. Also, fair warning: it'll suck. Enjoy.<br/><br/>First: <b>READ THE BOOKS IF YOU HAVEN'T YET, OKAY. I RECOMMEND THEM STRONGLY.</b><br/><br/>Second: *stares for another 4782 hours at the laptop screen beca</span>
  <span id="freeText17744541850214161299" style="display:none"><b>*yells for the next 10 years* THAT WAS JUST INCREDIBLE.</b><br /><br />I lowkey stared at my laptop screen for a long while before I actually started typing out my review. I was too shook to write a review for book one and I'm also shook about this one, but I feel the need to write one. Excuse me, it will basically consist of me yelling. Also, fair warning: it'll suck. Enjoy.<br /><br />First: <b>READ THE BOOKS IF YOU HAVEN'T YET, OKAY. I RECOMMEND THEM STRONGLY.</b><br /><br />Second: *stares for another 4782 hours at the laptop screen because I don't know how to start this?!?!* <br /><br />LOOK. I BINGED THE HELL OUT OF THIS TODAY. IT WAS THAT GOOD. I dedicated my day for it. I love the plot. I love the world. I love the characters (except King Gaius and Aron, they can go to hell). I love it ALL ALL ALL. <br /><br />My favorite character: Magnus Lukas Damora, ladies and gentleman. MY PRECIOUS LOST BABY. HE'S DEVELOPED SINCE BOOK ONE AND I LOVE IT. He's so confused and doesn't know what kind of person to be and baby, he's just so conflicted. I just want to protect him. #ProtectMagnusDamora<br /><br />ALSO. Cleo. Poor thing, she's suffered so much and I can't wait to see how she'll rise above everyone because she's badass and she can kick ass. Just you wait!<br /><br />Lucia is insane. I love her though. She's also confused and lost and scared. Poor baby. We didn't get too much Lucia chapters but I can't wait to see what Morgan Rhodes has in store for her character!<br /><br />Jonas, my messed up baby. Literally all his plans have a 0% success chance. He's impulsive and stubborn but I love him, okay. I get why he's like that, but Jonas, honey, chill.<br /><br />ALL IN ALL: I LOVE ALL THE MAINS. <br /><br />The plot is well... INCREDIBLE. I will not go into details because I just can't???? (Psssst, read the books). Also, Morgan Rhodes and her random, spontaneous deaths. They kill me. MORGAN, PLEASE. What's also funny is basically everyone's in love with everyone one way or another, but do I care? NOPE. I AM LIVING FOR IT, TOO. I LOVE EVERYTHING ABOUT THIS BOOK (except the pieces of shits King Gaius and Aron, again).<br /><br />THIS IS MY REVIEW, OK. IT SUCKS BUT I CAN'T DO IT. I'M TOO SKEAHJSDFJ. THIS IS ALL I CAN DO BECAUSE THIS BOOK IS TOO GOOD AND I CAN'T WRITE A COHERENT PROPER REVIEW. BYE. ALSO, READ THE BOOKS, DON'T FORGET.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17744541850214161299" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_782691335" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/782691335" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/782691335?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring">boring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=wtf">wtf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=wtfery">wtfery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=whiny-annoying-blah-heroine">whiny-annoying-blah-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=rubbish-worldbuilding">rubbish-worldbuilding</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=witchy-shit">witchy-shit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=meh">meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=unlikeable-characters">unlikeable-characters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer782691335" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8500792285254904519"><b>Spoilers</b><br/><br/>-I enjoyed <i>Rebel Spring</i> more than the first book, which I absolutely hated, I only read this for completion's sake. This was still mostly a rubbish book but it did at least have some entertaining moments.<br/><br/>-What's what: Evul King Gaius conquered Auranos/Paelasia. He now wants to gain ultimate power and immortality and do other cliched evul things. Naturally, a bunch of sexy teenagers have to stop him.<br/><br/>-There were too many cliched romances. Every character seemed to fall in love with anyone </span>
  <span id="freeText8500792285254904519" style="display:none"><b>Spoilers</b><br /><br />-I enjoyed <i>Rebel Spring</i> more than the first book, which I absolutely hated, I only read this for completion's sake. This was still mostly a rubbish book but it did at least have some entertaining moments.<br /><br />-What's what: Evul King Gaius conquered Auranos/Paelasia. He now wants to gain ultimate power and immortality and do other cliched evul things. Naturally, a bunch of sexy teenagers have to stop him.<br /><br />-There were too many cliched romances. Every character seemed to fall in love with anyone they spent five minutes with. None of the romances seemed believable.<br />I still don't get why a two thousand year old man would be lusting after a sixteen year old child-like teenage girl. It was perverted. <br /><br />-Magnus and Cleo were the only characters I was remotely invested in.<br /><br />-Lucia was a whiny-self-obsessed-pathetic-judgmental Mary Sue, I thought she was bad in the first book but she was even worse in this one. I hope she dies by the end of the series. <br /><br />-Cleo was the best character. I thought her being forced to marry Magnus would be boring but it was actually rather interesting. Their history (Magnus being a dick and killing her first love) just made their interactions all the more fun. It was quite sweet how they slowly developed feelings for each other, even though they didn't realise what was happening. I kind of hope they end up together.<br /><br />-Jonas was a judgmental prick. I hated him in the first book and I hate him even more now. Characters that constantly moan about the rich or people that live comfortably piss me off. Jonas acted like he had the right to judge everyone else just because he was poor. Ugh, he was a wanker.<br /> <br />-Magnus was a self-pitying emo bitch but his relationship with Cleo gave him some much needed dimensions. His feelings for his sister (Lucia) were still creepy, but I'm sure he's confusing romantic love with loving a sibling who has always been there for him. <br /><br />-Lysandra was annoying, she was basically a female Jonas. Someone who was constantly on their high horse acting like judge, jury, and executioner. Her horrid attitude towards Cleo was irritating, she thought because she was poor she had a monopoly on pain and that rich Cleo couldn't possibly understand or experience any kind of hardships - Cleo lost her whole family and was forced to live with her father's murderers, she went through hell but did Lysandra show any compassion or kindness? No, she acted like a cow to Cleo even though she didn't deserve it. Ugh.<br />Lysandra's romance with Jonas was cringey and came out of nowhere. I guess they both suited each other though since they were both douches.<br /><br />-King Gaius was so one dimensional and flat, he had no depth whatsoever. His ultimate plan was to gain immortality and power no matter how many lives he had to take, he didn't have one redeeming quality about him, someone that fucked up should have motivations behind their actions. But there was no reason behind his desires and needs, why was he so hellbent on getting power? Why was he so cool with death and destruction? He didn't even love his own children. Where was his layers? Ugh, I hate bad guys who have no depth at all.<br /><br />-There were too many POV's and too many love triangles.<br /><br />-All in all, most of this was rubbish but there were some moments (Cleo and Magnus's relationship mainly) that were enjoyable.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8500792285254904519" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('y4d6HQTsm+dwUHD+w5y8cYsdGO8Vdm1pKR5f653SsDQBIoElWU93NIp7dXmKPT1g2Yv9yY5i0qnjhfUTtCutWg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VkGJ3+r+w2UncpLw5ZmXquFJUTTfrSdfYd74gVjsbtqc5HLnt10vtt1Zl3esOBa7s9+0EkS5mJ+rRVJ5cRVztA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer10095465517791817751">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet vor</span>
  <span id="freeText10095465517791817751" style="display:none">Morgan Rhodes lives in Ontario, Canada. As a child, she always wanted to be a princess -- the kind that knows how to wield a sharp sword to help save both kingdoms and princes from fire-breathing dragons and dark wizards. Instead, she became a writer, which is just as good and much less dangerous. Along with writing, Morgan enjoys photography, travel, reality TV, and is an extremely picky, yet voracious reader of all kinds of books. Under another pen name, she’s a national bestselling author of many paranormal novels. Falling Kingdoms is her first high fantasy. </span>
